Line codes: 1 Name 2 Address 3 Country and Town 4 Date of Birth 5 Place of Birth 6 Customer Identification Number 7 National Idenitifty Number 8 Additional Information Edits: 1)Each LINE must begin with one of the numeric codes in numerical order. 2)Code 1 and 2 can be repeated, but codes 3,4,5,6,7 and 8 cannot be repeated. 3)Code 2 (Address) cannot be used with Code 3 (Country and Town) 4)Code 4(Date of Birth) cannot be used without Code 5(Place of Birth) and vice versa. 5)Code 8 can only be used to continue information from one of the following: The PARTY.IDENT when Unique Identifier Option is used. Code 6 (Customer Identification Number) Code 7 (National Identity Number) For e.g., using PARTY.LINE.1, PARTY.LINE.2 and PARTY.LINE.3 2/123 MAIN STREET 3/US/NEWYORK,NY 10000 7/123-45-6789

        public void insertPartyAddr(TField param, int pos)
        Insert the specified PartyAddr to the specified position in the collection.
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: If any of PARTY.ADDR.1 through PARTY.ADDR.3 is used, the line must begin with one of the following Line codes followed by a slash / and then followed by at least one non-space character. Line codes: 1 Name 2 Address 3 Country and Town 4 Date of Birth 5 Place of Birth 6 Customer Identification Number 7 National Idenitifty Number 8 Additional Information Edits: 1)Each LINE must begin with one of the numeric codes in numerical order. 2)Code 1 and 2 can be repeated, but codes 3,4,5,6,7 and 8 cannot be repeated. 3)Code 2 (Address) cannot be used with Code 3 (Country and Town) 4)Code 4(Date of Birth) cannot be used without Code 5(Place of Birth) and vice versa. 5)Code 8 can only be used to continue information from one of the following: The PARTY.IDENT when Unique Identifier Option is used. Code 6 (Customer Identification Number) Code 7 (National Identity Number) For e.g., using PARTY.LINE.1, PARTY.LINE.2 and PARTY.LINE.3 2/123 MAIN STREET 3/US/NEWYORK,NY 10000 7/123-45-6789
